You can find more information in the Wiki: \u003ca href=\"https://github.com/fastfetch-cli/fastfetch/wiki/Configuration\"\u003ehttps://github.com/fastfetch-cli/fastfetch/wiki/Configuration\u003c/a\u003e.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eFastfetch is more polished. For example, neofetch prints \u003ccode\u003e555 MiB\u003c/code\u003e in the Memory module and \u003ccode\u003e23 G\u003c/code\u003e in the Disk module, whereas fastfetch prints \u003ccode\u003e555.00 MiB\u003c/code\u003e and \u003ccode\u003e22.97 GiB\u003c/code\u003e respectively.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eFastfetch is more accurate. For example, \u003ca href=\"https://github.com/dylanaraps/neofetch/pull/2395\" data-hovercard-type=\"pull_request\" data-hovercard-url=\"/dylanaraps/neofetch/pull/2395/hovercard\"\u003eneofetch never actually supports the Wayland protocol\u003c/a\u003e.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ol\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch3 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\"\u003eQ: Fastfetch shows my local IP address. It only has meaning if you are on the same network, for example, if you connect to the same Wi-Fi network.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eActually, the \u003ccode\u003eLocal IP\u003c/code\u003e module is the most useful module for me personally. I (@CarterLi) have several VMs installed to test fastfetch and often need to SSH into them. With fastfetch running on shell startup, I never need to type \u003ccode\u003eip addr\u003c/code\u003e manually.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eIf you really don't like it, you can disable the \u003ccode\u003eLocal IP\u003c/code\u003e module in \u003ccode\u003econfig.jsonc\u003c/code\u003e.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch3 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\"\u003eQ: Where is the config file? <a href="https://deepwiki.com/fastfetch-cli/fastfetch" rel="nofollow"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/e7d4bb1a32530e373bb53fbe8eea825440ad27c7531d8f144d561acdd20c093a/68747470733a2f2f6465657077696b692e636f6d2f62616467652e737667" alt="Ask DeepWiki" data-canonical-src="https://deepwiki.com/badge.svg" style="max-width: 100%;"></a>
<a href="/fastfetch-cli/fastfetch/blob/dev/README-cn.md"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/ba7d79cac1e54cf92588ae67fefd65023ca931661496fc657e2c17f8811ef273/68747470733a2f2f696d672e736869656c64732e696f2f62616467652f2545342542382541442545362539362538372d524541444d452d726564" alt="README" data-canonical-src="https://img.shields.io/badge/%E4%B8%AD%E6%96%87-README-red" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">Fastfetch is a <a href="https://github.com/dylanaraps/neofetch">neofetch</a>-like tool for fetching system information and displaying it in a visually appealing way. It is written mainly in C, with a focus on performance and customizability. Currently, it supports Linux, macOS, Windows 7+, Android, FreeBSD, OpenBSD, NetBSD, DragonFly, Haiku, and SunOS.</p>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Installation</h2><a id="user-content-installation" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Installation" href="#installation"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Linux</h3><a id="user-content-linux" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Linux" href="#linux"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Some distributions package outdated versions of fastfetch. Older versions receive no support, so please always try to use the latest version.</p>
<a href="https://repology.org/project/fastfetch/versions" rel="nofollow">
    <img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/b5aef15e14de3a49d6b730b6ba7169b57a614c9eba756fb70a319e2ff11b05a1/68747470733a2f2f7265706f6c6f67792e6f72672f62616467652f766572746963616c2d616c6c7265706f732f6661737466657463682e7376673f636f6c756d6e733d32" alt="Packaging status" align="right" data-canonical-src="https://repology.org/badge/vertical-allrepos/fastfetch.svg?columns=2" style="max-width: 100%;">
</a>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Debian: <code>apt install fastfetch</code> (for Debian 13 or newer)</li>
<li>Debian / Ubuntu: Download <code>fastfetch-linux-&lt;proper architecture&gt;.deb</code> from <a href="https://github.com/fastfetch-cli/fastfetch/releases/latest">Github release page</a> and double-click it (for Ubuntu 20.04 or newer and Debian 11 or newer).</li>
<li>Arch Linux: <code>pacman -S fastfetch</code></li>
<li>Fedora: <code>dnf install fastfetch</code></li>
<li>Gentoo: <code>emerge --ask app-misc/fastfetch</code></li>
<li>Alpine: <code>apk add --upgrade fastfetch</code></li>
<li>NixOS: <code>nix-shell -p fastfetch</code></li>
<li>openSUSE: <code>zypper install fastfetch</code></li>
<li>ALT Linux: <code>apt-get install fastfetch</code></li>
<li>Exherbo: <code>cave resolve --execute app-misc/fastfetch</code></li>
<li>Solus: <code>eopkg install fastfetch</code></li>
<li>Slackware: <code>sbopkg -i fastfetch</code></li>
<li>Void Linux: <code>xbps-install fastfetch</code></li>
<li>Venom Linux: <code>scratch install fastfetch</code></li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">You may need <code>sudo</code>, <code>doas</code>, or <code>sup</code> to run these commands.</p>
<p dir="auto">If fastfetch is not packaged for your distribution or an outdated version is packaged, <a href="https://brew.sh/" rel="nofollow">linuxbrew</a> is a good alternative: <code>brew install fastfetch</code></p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">macOS</h3><a id="user-content-macos" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: macOS" href="#macos"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><a href="https://formulae.brew.sh/formula/fastfetch#default" rel="nofollow">Homebrew</a>: <code>brew install fastfetch</code></li>
<li><a href="https://ports.macports.org/port/fastfetch/" rel="nofollow">MacPorts</a>: <code>sudo port install fastfetch</code></li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Windows</h3><a id="user-content-windows" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Windows" href="#windows"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><a href="https://scoop.sh/#/apps?q=fastfetch" rel="nofollow">scoop</a>: <code>scoop install fastfetch</code></li>
<li><a href="https://community.chocolatey.org/packages/fastfetch" rel="nofollow">Chocolatey</a>: <code>choco install fastfetch</code></li>
<li><a href="https://github.com/microsoft/winget-pkgs/tree/master/manifests/f/Fastfetch-cli/Fastfetch">winget</a>: <code>winget install fastfetch</code></li>
<li><a href="https://packages.msys2.org/base/mingw-w64-fastfetch" rel="nofollow">MSYS2 MinGW</a>: <code>pacman -S mingw-w64-&lt;subsystem&gt;-&lt;arch&gt;-fastfetch</code></li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">You may also download the program directly from <a href="https://github.com/fastfetch-cli/fastfetch/releases/latest">the GitHub releases page</a> in the form of an archive file.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">BSD systems</h3><a id="user-content-bsd-systems" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: BSD systems" href="#bsd-systems"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>FreeBSD: <code>pkg install fastfetch</code></li>
<li>NetBSD: <code>pkgin in fastfetch</code></li>
<li>OpenBSD: <code>pkg_add fastfetch</code> (Snapshots only)</li>
<li>DragonFly BSD: <code>pkg install fastfetch</code> (Snapshots only)</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Android (Termux)</h3><a id="user-content-android-termux" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Android (Termux)" href="#android-termux"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Build from source</h2><a id="user-content-build-from-source" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Build from source" href="#build-from-source"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">See the Wiki: <a href="https://github.com/fastfetch-cli/fastfetch/wiki/Building">https://github.com/fastfetch-cli/fastfetch/wiki/Building</a></p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Usage</h2><a id="user-content-usage" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Usage" href="#usage"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Run with default configuration: <code>fastfetch</code></li>
<li>Run with <a href="https://github.com/fastfetch-cli/fastfetch/wiki/Support+Status#available-modules">all supported modules</a> to find what interests you: <code>fastfetch -c all.jsonc</code></li>
<li>View all data that fastfetch detects: <code>fastfetch -s &lt;module1&gt;[:&lt;module2&gt;][:&lt;module3&gt;] --format json</code></li>
<li>Display help messages: <code>fastfetch --help</code></li>
<li>Generate a minimal config file: <code>fastfetch [-s &lt;module1&gt;[:&lt;module2&gt;]] --gen-config [&lt;/path/to/config.jsonc&gt;]</code>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Use: <code>--gen-config-full</code> to generate a full config file with all optional options</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Customization</h2><a id="user-content-customization" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Customization" href="#customization"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Fastfetch uses JSONC (JSON with comments) for configuration. <a href="https://github.com/fastfetch-cli/fastfetch/wiki/Configuration">See the Wiki for details</a>. There are some premade config files in the <a href="/fastfetch-cli/fastfetch/blob/dev/presets"><code>presets</code></a> directory, including those used for the screenshots above. You can load them using <code>-c &lt;filename&gt;</code>. These files can serve as examples of the configuration syntax.</p>
<p dir="auto">Logos can also be heavily customized; see the <a href="https://github.com/fastfetch-cli/fastfetch/wiki/Logo-options">logo documentation</a> for more information.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">WARNING</h3><a id="user-content-warning" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: WARNING" href="#warning"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Fastfetch supports a <code>Command</code> module that can run arbitrary shell commands. If you copy-paste a config file from an untrusted source, it may contain malicious commands that can harm your system or compromise your privacy. Please always review the config file before using it.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">FAQ</h2><a id="user-content-faq" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: FAQ" href="#faq"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Q: Neofetch is good enough. Why do I need fastfetch?</h3><a id="user-content-q-neofetch-is-good-enough-why-do-i-need-fastfetch" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Q: Neofetch is good enough. Why do I need fastfetch?" href="#q-neofetch-is-good-enough-why-do-i-need-fastfetch"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>Fastfetch is actively maintained.</li>
<li>Fastfetch is faster, as the name suggests.</li>
<li>Fastfetch has a greater number of features, though by default it only has a few modules enabled; use <code>fastfetch -c all</code> to discover what you want.</li>
<li>Fastfetch is more configurable. You can find more information in the Wiki: <a href="https://github.com/fastfetch-cli/fastfetch/wiki/Configuration">https://github.com/fastfetch-cli/fastfetch/wiki/Configuration</a>.</li>
<li>Fastfetch is more polished. For example, neofetch prints <code>555 MiB</code> in the Memory module and <code>23 G</code> in the Disk module, whereas fastfetch prints <code>555.00 MiB</code> and <code>22.97 GiB</code> respectively.</li>
<li>Fastfetch is more accurate. For example, <a href="https://github.com/dylanaraps/neofetch/pull/2395" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/dylanaraps/neofetch/pull/2395/hovercard">neofetch never actually supports the Wayland protocol</a>.</li>
</ol>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Q: Fastfetch shows my local IP address. Does it leak my privacy?</h3><a id="user-content-q-fastfetch-shows-my-local-ip-address-does-it-leak-my-privacy" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Q: Fastfetch shows my local IP address. Does it leak my privacy?" href="#q-fastfetch-shows-my-local-ip-address-does-it-leak-my-privacy"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">A local IP address (10.x.x.x, 172.x.x.x, 192.168.x.x) has nothing to do with privacy. It only has meaning if you are on the same network, for example, if you connect to the same Wi-Fi network.</p>
<p dir="auto">Actually, the <code>Local IP</code> module is the most useful module for me personally. I (@CarterLi) have several VMs installed to test fastfetch and often need to SSH into them. With fastfetch running on shell startup, I never need to type <code>ip addr</code> manually.</p>
<p dir="auto">If you really don't like it, you can disable the <code>Local IP</code> module in <code>config.jsonc</code>.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Q: Where is the config file? I can't find it.</h3><a id="user-content-q-where-is-the-config-file-i-cant-find-it" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Q: Where is the config file? I can't find it." href="#q-where-is-the-config-file-i-cant-find-it"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Fastfetch does not generate a config file automatically. You can use <code>fastfetch --gen-config</code> to generate one. The config file will be saved in <code>~/.config/fastfetch/config.jsonc</code> by default. See the <a href="https://github.com/fastfetch-cli/fastfetch/wiki/Configuration">Wiki for details</a>.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Q: The configuration is so complex. Where is the documentation?</h3><a id="user-content-q-the-configuration-is-so-complex-where-is-the-documentation" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Q: The configuration is so complex. Where is the documentation?" href="#q-the-configuration-is-so-complex-where-is-the-documentation"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Fastfetch uses JSON (with comments) for configuration. I suggest using an IDE with JSON schema support (like VSCode) to edit it.</p>
<p dir="auto">Alternatively, you can refer to the presets in the <a href="https://github.com/fastfetch-cli/fastfetch/tree/dev/presets"><code>presets</code> directory</a>.</p>
<p dir="auto">The <strong>correct</strong> way to edit the configuration:</p>
<p dir="auto">This is an example that <a href="https://github.com/fastfetch-cli/fastfetch/discussions/1014" data-hovercard-type="discussion" data-hovercard-url="/fastfetch-cli/fastfetch/discussions/1014/hovercard">changes size prefix from MiB / GiB to MB / GB</a>. Editor used: <a href="https://github.com/helix-editor/helix">helix</a></p>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://asciinema.org/a/1uF6sTPGKrHKI1MVaFcikINSQ" rel="nofollow"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/15f03ba43ff8af9a04cbf3a04433acf1ddea15092aace6109fba5694c166c7f2/68747470733a2f2f61736369696e656d612e6f72672f612f31754636735450474b72484b49314d56614663696b494e53512e737667" alt="asciicast" data-canonical-src="https://asciinema.org/a/1uF6sTPGKrHKI1MVaFcikINSQ.svg" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Q: I WANT THE DOCUMENTATION!</h3><a id="user-content-q-i-want-the-documentation" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Q: I WANT THE DOCUMENTATION!" href="#q-i-want-the-documentation"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/fastfetch-cli/fastfetch/wiki/Json-Schema">Here is the documentation</a>. It is generated from the <a href="https://github.com/fastfetch-cli/fastfetch/blob/dev/doc/json_schema.json">JSON schema</a>, but you might not find it very user-friendly.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Q: How can I customize the module output?</h3><a id="user-content-q-how-can-i-customize-the-module-output" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Q: How can I customize the module output?" href="#q-how-can-i-customize-the-module-output"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Fastfetch uses <code>format</code> to generate output. For example, to make the <code>GPU</code> module show only the GPU name (leaving other information undisplayed), you can use:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-json-comments notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="{
    &quot;modules&quot;: [
        {
            &quot;type&quot;: &quot;gpu&quot;,
            &quot;format&quot;: &quot;{name}&quot; // See `fastfetch -h gpu-format` for details
        }
    ]
}"><pre>{
    <span class="pl-ent">"modules"</span>: [
        {
            <span class="pl-ent">"type"</span>: <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>gpu<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,
            <span class="pl-ent">"format"</span>: <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>{name}<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> See `fastfetch -h gpu-format` for details</span>
        }
    ]
}</pre></div>
<p dir="auto">...which is equivalent to <code>fastfetch -s gpu --gpu-format '{name}'</code></p>
<p dir="auto">See <code>fastfetch -h format</code> for information on basic usage. For module-specific formatting, see <code>fastfetch -h &lt;module&gt;-format</code></p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Q: I have my own ASCII art / image file. How can I show it with fastfetch?</h3><a id="user-content-q-i-have-my-own-ascii-art--image-file-how-can-i-show-it-with-fastfetch" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Q: I have my own ASCII art / image file. How can I show it with fastfetch?" href="#q-i-have-my-own-ascii-art--image-file-how-can-i-show-it-with-fastfetch"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Try <code>fastfetch -l /path/to/logo</code>. See the <a href="https://github.com/fastfetch-cli/fastfetch/wiki/Logo-options">logo documentation</a> for details.</p>
<p dir="auto">If you just want to display the distro name in <a href="https://github.com/pwaller/pyfiglet">FIGlet text</a>:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="# install pyfiglet and jq first
pyfiglet -s -f small_slant $(fastfetch -s os --format json | jq -r '.[0].result.name') &amp;&amp; fastfetch -l none"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> install pyfiglet and jq first</span>
pyfiglet -s -f small_slant <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$(</span>fastfetch -s os --format json <span class="pl-k">|</span> jq -r <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>.[0].result.name<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span><span class="pl-pds">)</span></span> <span class="pl-k">&amp;&amp;</span> fastfetch -l none</pre></div>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="https://private-user-images.githubusercontent.com/6134068/333780073-6466524e-ab8c-484f-848d-eec7ddeb7df2.png?jwt=eyJ0eXAiOiJKV1QiLCJhbGciOiJIUzI1NiJ9.eyJpc3MiOiJnaXRodWIuY29tIiwiYXVkIjoicmF3LmdpdGh1YnVzZXJjb250ZW50LmNvbSIsImtleSI6ImtleTUiLCJleHAiOjE3NjI4MTU1NTcsIm5iZiI6MTc2MjgxNTI1NywicGF0aCI6Ii82MTM0MDY4LzMzMzc4MDA3My02NDY2NTI0ZS1hYjhjLTQ4NGYtODQ4ZC1lZWM3ZGRlYjdkZjIucG5nP1gtQW16LUFsZ29yaXRobT1BV1M0LUhNQUMtU0hBMjU2JlgtQW16LUNyZWRlbnRpYWw9QUtJQVZDT0RZTFNBNTNQUUs0WkElMkYyMDI1MTExMCUyRnVzLWVhc3QtMSUyRnMzJTJGYXdzNF9yZXF1ZXN0JlgtQW16LURhdGU9MjAyNTExMTBUMjI1NDE3WiZYLUFtei1FeHBpcmVzPTMwMCZYLUFtei1TaWduYXR1cmU9NDM5MDhjN2ExZTlhODYyNzBlMjVlM2MzODNmNjViMmFlNTYxMTZjYjMxYWM4MGM5NDc0MDkyYmMzMjY2NzRhNSZYLUFtei1TaWduZWRIZWFkZXJzPWhvc3QifQ.r2zL2GJw7cLldievvW2HoSOB7U5zzS5HWAETSWzHiAQ"><img src="https://private-user-images.githubusercontent.com/6134068/333780073-6466524e-ab8c-484f-848d-eec7ddeb7df2.png?jwt=eyJ0eXAiOiJKV1QiLCJhbGciOiJIUzI1NiJ9.eyJpc3MiOiJnaXRodWIuY29tIiwiYXVkIjoicmF3LmdpdGh1YnVzZXJjb250ZW50LmNvbSIsImtleSI6ImtleTUiLCJleHAiOjE3NjI4MTU1NTcsIm5iZiI6MTc2MjgxNTI1NywicGF0aCI6Ii82MTM0MDY4LzMzMzc4MDA3My02NDY2NTI0ZS1hYjhjLTQ4NGYtODQ4ZC1lZWM3ZGRlYjdkZjIucG5nP1gtQW16LUFsZ29yaXRobT1BV1M0LUhNQUMtU0hBMjU2JlgtQW16LUNyZWRlbnRpYWw9QUtJQVZDT0RZTFNBNTNQUUs0WkElMkYyMDI1MTExMCUyRnVzLWVhc3QtMSUyRnMzJTJGYXdzNF9yZXF1ZXN0JlgtQW16LURhdGU9MjAyNTExMTBUMjI1NDE3WiZYLUFtei1FeHBpcmVzPTMwMCZYLUFtei1TaWduYXR1cmU9NDM5MDhjN2ExZTlhODYyNzBlMjVlM2MzODNmNjViMmFlNTYxMTZjYjMxYWM4MGM5NDc0MDkyYmMzMjY2NzRhNSZYLUFtei1TaWduZWRIZWFkZXJzPWhvc3QifQ.r2zL2GJw7cLldievvW2HoSOB7U5zzS5HWAETSWzHiAQ" alt="image" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Q: My image logo behaves strangely. How can I fix it?</h3><a id="user-content-q-my-image-logo-behaves-strangely-how-can-i-fix-it" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Q: My image logo behaves strangely. <p dir="auto">See the troubleshooting section: <a href="https://github.com/fastfetch-cli/fastfetch/wiki/Logo-options#troubleshooting">https://github.com/fastfetch-cli/fastfetch/wiki/Logo-options#troubleshooting</a></p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Q: Fastfetch runs in black and white on shell startup. Why?</h3><a id="user-content-q-fastfetch-runs-in-black-and-white-on-shell-startup-why" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Q: Fastfetch runs in black and white on shell startup. Why?" href="#q-fastfetch-runs-in-black-and-white-on-shell-startup-why"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">This issue usually occurs when using fastfetch with <code>p10k</code>. There are known incompatibilities between fastfetch and p10k instant prompt.
The p10k documentation clearly states that you should NOT print anything to stdout after <code>p10k-instant-prompt</code> is initialized. You should put <code>fastfetch</code> before the initialization of <code>p10k-instant-prompt</code> (recommended).</p>
<p dir="auto">You can always use <code>fastfetch --pipe false</code> to force fastfetch to run in colorful mode.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Q: Why do fastfetch and neofetch show different memory usage results?</h3><a id="user-content-q-why-do-fastfetch-and-neofetch-show-different-memory-usage-results" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Q: Why do fastfetch and neofetch show different memory usage results?" href="#q-why-do-fastfetch-and-neofetch-show-different-memory-usage-results"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">See <a href="https://github.com/fastfetch-cli/fastfetch/issues/1096" data-hovercard-type="issue" data-hovercard-url="/fastfetch-cli/fastfetch/issues/1096/hovercard">#1096</a>.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Q: Fastfetch shows fewer dpkg packages than neofetch. Is it a bug?</h3><a id="user-content-q-fastfetch-shows-fewer-dpkg-packages-than-neofetch-is-it-a-bug" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Q: Fastfetch shows fewer dpkg packages than neofetch. Is it a bug?" href="#q-fastfetch-shows-fewer-dpkg-packages-than-neofetch-is-it-a-bug"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Neofetch incorrectly counts <code>rc</code> packages (packages that have been removed but still have configuration files remaining). See bug: <a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="1522884894" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/dylanaraps/neofetch/issues/2278" data-hovercard-type="issue" data-hovercard-url="/dylanaraps/neofetch/issues/2278/hovercard" href="https://github.com/dylanaraps/neofetch/issues/2278">dylanaraps/neofetch#2278</a></p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Q: I use Debian / Ubuntu / Debian-derived distro. My GPU is detected as <code>XXXX Device XXXX (VGA compatible)</code>. Is this a bug?</h3><a id="user-content-q-i-use-debian--ubuntu--debian-derived-distro-my-gpu-is-detected-as-xxxx-device-xxxx-vga-compatible-is-this-a-bug" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Q: I use Debian / Ubuntu / Debian-derived distro. My GPU is detected as XXXX Device XXXX (VGA compatible). Is this a bug?" href="#q-i-use-debian--ubuntu--debian-derived-distro-my-gpu-is-detected-as-xxxx-device-xxxx-vga-compatible-is-this-a-bug"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Try upgrading <code>pci.ids</code>: Download <a href="https://pci-ids.ucw.cz/v2.2/pci.ids" rel="nofollow">https://pci-ids.ucw.cz/v2.2/pci.ids</a> and overwrite the file <code>/usr/share/hwdata/pci.ids</code>. For AMD GPUs, you should also upgrade <code>amdgpu.ids</code>: Download <a href="https://gitlab.freedesktop.org/mesa/drm/-/raw/main/data/amdgpu.ids" rel="nofollow">https://gitlab.freedesktop.org/mesa/drm/-/raw/main/data/amdgpu.ids</a> and overwrite the file <code>/usr/share/libdrm/amdgpu.ids</code></p>
<p dir="auto">Alternatively, you may try using <code>fastfetch --gpu-driver-specific</code>, which will make fastfetch attempt to ask the driver for the GPU name if supported.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Q: I get the error <code>Authorization required, but no authorization protocol specified</code> when running fastfetch as root</h3><a id="user-content-q-i-get-the-error-authorization-required-but-no-authorization-protocol-specified-when-running-fastfetch-as-root" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Q: I get the error Authorization required, but no authorization protocol specified when running fastfetch as root" href="#q-i-get-the-error-authorization-required-but-no-authorization-protocol-specified-when-running-fastfetch-as-root"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Try <code>export XAUTHORITY=$HOME/.Xauthority</code></p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Q: Fastfetch cannot detect my awesome 3rd-party macOS window manager!</h3><a id="user-content-q-fastfetch-cannot-detect-my-awesome-3rd-party-macos-window-manager" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Q: Fastfetch cannot detect my awesome 3rd-party macOS window manager!" href="#q-fastfetch-cannot-detect-my-awesome-3rd-party-macos-window-manager"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Q: How can I change the colors of my ASCII logo?</h3><a id="user-content-q-how-can-i-change-the-colors-of-my-ascii-logo" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Q: How can I change the colors of my ASCII logo?" href="#q-how-can-i-change-the-colors-of-my-ascii-logo"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Try <code>fastfetch --logo-color-[1-9] &lt;color&gt;</code>, where <code>[1-9]</code> is the index of color placeholders.</p>
<p dir="auto">For example: <code>fastfetch --logo-color-1 red --logo-color-2 green</code>.</p>
<p dir="auto">In JSONC, you can use:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-json-comments notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="{
    &quot;logo&quot;: {
        &quot;color&quot;: {
            &quot;1&quot;: &quot;red&quot;,
            &quot;2&quot;: &quot;green&quot;
        }
    }
}"><pre>{
    <span class="pl-ent">"logo"</span>: {
        <span class="pl-ent">"color"</span>: {
            <span class="pl-ent">"1"</span>: <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>red<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,
            <span class="pl-ent">"2"</span>: <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>green<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>
        }
    }
}</pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Q: How do I hide a key?</h3><a id="user-content-q-how-do-i-hide-a-key" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Q: How do I hide a key?" href="#q-how-do-i-hide-a-key"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Set the key to a white space.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-json-comments notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="{
    &quot;key&quot;: &quot; &quot;
}"><pre>{
    <span class="pl-ent">"key"</span>: <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span> <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>
}</pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Q: How can I display images on Windows?</h3><a id="user-content-q-how-can-i-display-images-on-windows" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Q: How can I display images on Windows?" href="#q-how-can-i-display-images-on-windows"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">As of April 2025:</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">mintty and Wezterm</h4><a id="user-content-mintty-and-wezterm" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: mintty and Wezterm" href="#mintty-and-wezterm"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">mintty (used by Bash on Windows and MSYS2) and Wezterm (nightly build only) support the iTerm image protocol on Windows.</p>
<p dir="auto">In <code>config.jsonc</code>:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-json notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="{
  &quot;logo&quot;: {
    &quot;type&quot;: &quot;iterm&quot;,
    &quot;source&quot;: &quot;C:/path/to/image.png&quot;,
    &quot;width&quot;: &lt;num-in-chars&gt;
  }
}"><pre>{
  <span class="pl-ent">"logo"</span>: {
    <span class="pl-ent">"type"</span>: <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>iterm<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,
    <span class="pl-ent">"source"</span>: <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>C:/path/to/image.png<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,
    <span class="pl-ent">"width"</span>: <span class="pl-ii">&lt;num-in-chars&gt;</span>
  }
}</pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Windows Terminal</h4><a id="user-content-windows-terminal" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Windows Terminal" href="#windows-terminal"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Windows Terminal supports the sixel image protocol only.</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>If you installed fastfetch through MSYS2:
<ol dir="auto">
<li>Install imagemagick: <code>pacman -S mingw-w64-&lt;subsystem&gt;-x86_64-imagemagick</code></li>
<li>In <code>config.jsonc</code>:</li>
</ol>
</li>
</ul>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-json-comments notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="{
  &quot;logo&quot;: {
    &quot;type&quot;: &quot;sixel&quot;, // DO NOT USE &quot;auto&quot;
    &quot;source&quot;: &quot;C:/path/to/image.png&quot;, // Do NOT use `~` as fastfetch is a native Windows program and doesn't apply cygwin path conversion
    &quot;width&quot;: &lt;image-width-in-chars&gt;, // Optional
    &quot;height&quot;: &lt;image-height-in-chars&gt; // Optional
  }
}"><pre>{
  <span class="pl-ent">"logo"</span>: {
    <span class="pl-ent">"type"</span>: <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>sixel<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>, <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> DO NOT USE "auto"</span>
    <span class="pl-ent">"source"</span>: <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>C:/path/to/image.png<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>, <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> Do NOT use `~` as fastfetch is a native Windows program and doesn't apply cygwin path conversion</span>
    <span class="pl-ent">"width"</span>: <span class="pl-ii">&lt;image-width-in-chars&gt;</span>, <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> Optional</span>
    <span class="pl-ent">"height"</span>: <span class="pl-ii">&lt;image-height-in-chars&gt;</span> <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> Optional</span>
  }
}</pre></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>If you installed fastfetch via scoop or downloaded the binary directly from the GitHub Releases page:
<ol dir="auto">
<li>Convert your image manually to sixel format using <a href="https://www.google.com/search?q=convert+image+to+sixel" rel="nofollow">any online image conversion service</a></li>
<li>In <code>config.jsonc</code>:</li>
</ol>
</li>
</ul>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-json-comments notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="{
  &quot;logo&quot;: {
    &quot;type&quot;: &quot;raw&quot;, // DO NOT USE &quot;auto&quot;
    &quot;source&quot;: &quot;C:/path/to/image.sixel&quot;,
    &quot;width&quot;: &lt;image-width-in-chars&gt;, // Required
    &quot;height&quot;: &lt;image-height-in-chars&gt; // Required
  }
}"><pre>{
  <span class="pl-ent">"logo"</span>: {
    <span class="pl-ent">"type"</span>: <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>raw<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>, <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> DO NOT USE "auto"</span>
    <span class="pl-ent">"source"</span>: <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>C:/path/to/image.sixel<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,
    <span class="pl-ent">"width"</span>: <span class="pl-ii">&lt;image-width-in-chars&gt;</span>, <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> Required</span>
    <span class="pl-ent">"height"</span>: <span class="pl-ii">&lt;image-height-in-chars&gt;</span> <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> Required</span>
  }
}</pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Q: I want feature A / B / C. Will fastfetch support it?</h3><a id="user-content-q-i-want-feature-a--b--c-will-fastfetch-support-it" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Q: I want feature A / B / C. Will fastfetch support it?" href="#q-i-want-feature-a--b--c-will-fastfetch-support-it"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Fastfetch is a system information tool. We only accept hardware or system-level software feature requests. For most personal uses, I recommend using the <code>Command</code> module to implement custom functionality, which can be used to grab output from a custom shell script:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-json-comments notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// This module shows the default editor
{
    &quot;modules&quot;: [
        {
            &quot;type&quot;: &quot;command&quot;,
            &quot;text&quot;: &quot;$EDITOR --version | head -1&quot;,
            &quot;key&quot;: &quot;Editor&quot;
        }
    ]
}"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> This module shows the default editor</span>
{
    <span class="pl-ent">"modules"</span>: [
        {
            <span class="pl-ent">"type"</span>: <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>command<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,
            <span class="pl-ent">"text"</span>: <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>$EDITOR --version | head -1<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,
            <span class="pl-ent">"key"</span>: <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Editor<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>
        }
    ]
}</pre></div>
<p dir="auto">Otherwise, please open a feature request in <a href="https://github.com/fastfetch-cli/fastfetch/issues">GitHub Issues</a>.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Q: I have questions. Where can I get help?</h3><a id="user-content-q-i-have-questions-where-can-i-get-help" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Q: I have questions. Where can I get help?" href="#q-i-have-questions-where-can-i-get-help"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>For usage questions, please start a discussion in <a href="https://github.com/fastfetch-cli/fastfetch/discussions">GitHub Discussions</a>.</li>
<li>For possible bugs, please open an issue in <a href="https://github.com/fastfetch-cli/fastfetch/issues">GitHub Issues</a>. Be sure to fill out the bug report template carefully to help developers investigate.</li>
</ul>
